<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a> (75758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">gerbille</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gerbo</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">Ø¬ÙØ±Ù’Ø¨ÙÙˆØ¹</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarbÅ«Ê¿</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">ÙŠÙØ±Ù’Ø¨ÙÙˆØ¹</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yarbÅ«Ê¿</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">jerboa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gerbils</b>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gerbil" class="extiw" title="w:gerbil"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gerbil" class="extiw" title="w:gerbil">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li>One of several species of small, <a href = vnd.unilang:jumping.html>jumping</a>, murine rodents, of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gerbillus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gerbillus"><i>Gerbillus</i></a></span> and certain other genera in subfamily Gerbillinae, with leaping powers resembling the jerboa, native to Africa, India, and Southern Europe.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerbil.html>gerbil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gerbils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbilling</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbiling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbilled</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gerbiled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rotate inside a monowheel or similar apparatus due to sudden acceleration or braking.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To insert a small animal into one's <a href = vnd.unilang:rectum.html>rectum</a> (a sexual practice in urban myth).</li></ol>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <i>Gerbillinae</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondersoort.html>ondersoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a> <i>Muridae</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarnaast.html>daarnaast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muizen.html>muizen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ratten.html>ratten</a>, stekelmuizen <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwanten.html>verwanten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omvat.html>omvat</a></li></ol>

***gerecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a> (5968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gerichte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechte.html>gerechte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">court of law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gerihte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garihtijÄ…</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">something prepared or arranged</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gerihte</i>. The sense "dish" developed independently already in Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gerihte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">meal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechten.html>gerechten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerechtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> justice; the judiciary</li>
<li>court of law</li>
<li>a meal, or a dish served alone or part of a meal as a course</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gherecht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gereht</i> (in <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gerehto</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garehtaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">ğŒ²ğŒ°ğ‚ğŒ°ğŒ¹ğŒ·ğ„ğƒ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">garaihts</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">geriht</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtigd.html>gerechtigd</a> (42263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtigd.html>gerechtigd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtigd.html>gerechtigder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gerechtigdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">entitled</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">having a legal right to something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> AOW-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtigd.html>gerechtigd</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am not yet <b>entitled</b> to a Dutch state old-age pension.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gereed.html>gereed</a> (2210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gereet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*girÄ“de</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garaidijaz</i>, prefixed form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raidijaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raidaz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerief.html>gerief</a> (25796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gerijf</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerief.html>gerief</a></i>. Possibly derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rive</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rieve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">abundant, mild</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the prefix ge-, from uncertain origin. Possibly ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rÄ«baz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">generous, abundant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">riebus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">fat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerief.html>gerief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)

***gerst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerst.html>gerst</a> (36093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gerste</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gersta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*gerstu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gerst.html>gerst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>barley, <i>Hordeum vulgare</i></li>
<li>barley seed, used for brewing <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> separate, distinct
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probeer.html>probeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoonlijk.html>persoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gescheiden.html>gescheiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>.</i>

***geschiedenis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a> (1295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geschieden.html>geschieden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Geschichte</i>.
</p>
